<style>
  /* Force full-bleed container even inside boxed layouts */
  .mvb-bleed {
    width: 100vw;
    margin-left: calc(50% - 50vw);
    margin-right: calc(50% - 50vw);
    line-height: 0; /* kill any inline gaps */
  }

  /* Hero size: maintain 1920x768 ratio up to a max height of 768px */
  .mvb-hero {
    width: 100%;
    position: relative;
    height: min(calc(100vw * 0.4), 720px); /* <= key change */
    margin: 0 !important; padding: 0 !important;
  }

  /* Make Swiper fill the fixed height */
  .mvb-hero .swiper-wrapper,
  .mvb-hero .swiper-slide { height: 100%; }

  /* Slides + images */
  .mvb-hero .swiper-slide { display:flex; align-items:stretch; }
  .mvb-hero img { width:100%; height:100%; object-fit:cover; object-position:center; display:block; }

  /* Only show pointer on clickable slides */
  .mvb-slide--link { cursor:pointer; }

  /* Arrows + pagination colors */

class="fullSection none noBorder radius0 none c-section c-wrapper section-yzwqNdI_fS desktop-only mobile-only" style="" id="section-yzwqNdI_fS"><!----><!----><div class="inner"><!----><!--[--><!--[--><div class="row-align-center noBorder radius0 none c-row c-wrapper row-FKl2mFLyfI" id="row-FKl2mFLyfI"><!----><!----><div class="inner"><!----><!--[--><!--[--><div 255)">Programs for Athletes of All Ages &amp; class="fullSection noBorder radius0 none c-section c-wrapper section-CL-JUuc3yb" style="" id="section-CL-JUuc3yb"><div class="bg bgCover bg-section-CL-JUuc3yb none" style="border-radius:-2px;position:absolute;top:0;left:0;width:100%;height:100%;pointer-events:none;"></div><!----><div class="inner"><!----><!--[--><!--[--><div class="row-align-center noBorder radius0 none c-row c-wrapper row-D4-NbW-HJA" id="row-D4-NbW-HJA"><!----><!----><div class="inner"><!----><!--[--><!--[--><div class="noBorder radius0 none c-column c-wrapper col-3KPNhYPorT" id="col-3KPNhYPorT"><div class="bg bgCover bg-col-3KPNhYPorT none" style="border-radius:-3px;position:absolute;top:0;left:0;width:100%;height:100%;pointer-events:none;"></div><!----><div class="vertical inner"><!----><!--[--><!--[--><div id="heading-6O3UnHRvs_" class="c-heading c-wrapper"><!----><!----><!----><div class="heading-6O3UnHRvs_ text-output cheading-6O3UnHRvs_ noBorder radius0 none" data-animation-class style=""><div><h1><span style="color: rgb(254, 7, 78)">Upcoming Featured Programs</span></h1></div></div><!----><!----><!----><span></span><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----></div><!--]--><!--[--><div id="custom-code-r2tmbr-jHt" class="c-custom-code c-wrapper custom-code-r2tmbr-jHt"><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><span></span><div id="custom-code-r2tmbr-jHt" class="custom-code-container ccustom-code-r2tmbr-jHt"><script src="https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/npm/dayjs@1/dayjs.min.js"></script>

<script>
(function () {
  function buildUrlWithParams(locationId, params) {
    const searchParams = new URLSearchParams(params);
    const queryString = searchParams.toString();
    return `https://data.mmao.ca/ghlLeagues/${locationId}` + (queryString ? `?${queryString}` : '');
  }
  const currentVer = Date.now();
  const params = {
  ver: currentVer, 
  highlighted: "yes"
};
  const dataUrl = buildUrlWithParams("aGagGPzv1aS4v8hffakm",params);
  console.log('calling url', dataUrl);
  const textColor = "#fff";
  const loadingText = "Loading...";
  const noProgramsText = "No Programs";
  const SUFFIX = Date.now().toString(36) + Math.floor(Math.random() * 1e6).toString(36);
  const CONTAINER_ID = "program-results-" + SUFFIX;

  const here = document.currentScript;
  const container = document.createElement("div");
  container.id = CONTAINER_ID;
  container.style.padding = "20px";
  container.style.fontFamily = "'Roboto', sans-serif";
  container.style.color = textColor;
  container.textContent = loadingText;
  here.parentNode.insertBefore(container, here);

  // === 2) Local helpers (scoped; no globals) ===
  function formatDate(str) {
    return str ? dayjs(str).format("MMM D, YYYY") : "";
  }
  function parseDate(str) {
    if (!str) return null;
    return new Date(str + "T00:00:00");
  }
  function formatLabel(text) {
    return `<span style="margin-top: 4px; padding-left: 10px;font-size: 12px; color: #fff; font-style: italic;">${text}</span>`;
  }
  function format2fieldsTime(hour, minute) {
    let h = parseInt(hour ?? 0, 10);
    let m = String(minute ?? 0).padStart(2, "0");
    const ampm = h >= 12 ? "PM" : "AM";
    h = h % 12;
    if (h === 0) h = 12;
    return `${h}:${m} ${ampm}`;
  }

  // === 3) Unique global fns for this instance ===
  window["toggleAccordion_" + SUFFIX] = function (id) {
    const el = document.getElementById(id);
    if (!el) return;
    el.style.display = el.style.display === "none" ? "block" : "none";
  };
  window["toggleInnerAccordion_" + SUFFIX] = function (id) {
    const el = document.getElementById(id);
    if (!el) return;
    el.style.display = el.style.display === "none" ? "block" : "none";
  };

  window["loadPrograms_" + SUFFIX] = async function () {
    const container = document.getElementById(CONTAINER_ID);
    if (!container) return;

    const response = await fetch(dataUrl);
    const { records } = await response.json();

    if (!records || !Array.isArray(records) || !records.length) {
      container.innerHTML = '<p style="color:#fff;">'+noProgramsText+'</p>';
      return;
    }

    try {
      console.log('test 1');
      const groupedByCity = {};
      for (const record of records) {
        const city = record?.locationObject?.record?.properties?.city || "Unknown City";
        const programName = record.programObject?.record?.properties?.program_name || "Unnamed Program";
        groupedByCity[city] ??= {};
        groupedByCity[city][programName] ??= [];
        groupedByCity[city][programName].push(record);
      }
      console.log('test 2');
      for (const city in groupedByCity) {
        for (const programName in groupedByCity[city]) {
          groupedByCity[city][programName].sort((a, b) => {
            const dateA = parseDate(a.properties?.session_start_date) || 0;
            const dateB = parseDate(b.properties?.session_start_date) || 0;
            return dateA - dateB;
          });
        }
      }

      const output = Object.entries(groupedByCity)
        .map(([cityName, programs]) => {
          const programBlocks = Object.entries(programs)
            .map(([programName, groupItems]) => {
                const programInfo = groupItems[0]?.programObject?.record?.properties?.program_information || "";
              const itemsHTML = groupItems
                .map((item, index) => {
                  const sessionProperties = item.properties || {};
                  const programProperties = item.programObject?.record?.properties || {};
                  const locationProperties = item.locationObject?.record?.properties || {};

                  const slotsFilled = Array.isArray(item.relations)
                    ? item.relations.filter(s => s.objectKey === "custom_objects.youth").length
                    : 0;
                  const slotsAvailable = sessionProperties.session_capacity ?? 0;

                  const info = sessionProperties.session_information || "";
                  const cost = sessionProperties.session_cost || "";

                  const startDate = parseDate(sessionProperties.session_start_date);
                  const endDate = parseDate(sessionProperties.session_end_date);
                  const startVisible = parseDate(sessionProperties.session_start_date__visible_on_site) || startDate;
                  const endVisible = parseDate(sessionProperties.session_end_date__visible_on_site) || endDate;

                  const now = new Date();
                  const nextWeek = new Date(); nextWeek.setDate(now.getDate() + 7);

                  let dateOnlyStr = endDate
                    ? `${formatDate(sessionProperties.session_start_date)} – ${formatDate(sessionProperties.session_end_date)}`
                    : `${formatDate(sessionProperties.session_start_date)}`;
                    if(sessionProperties.session_start_date === sessionProperties.session_end_date) {
                        dateOnlyStr = formatDate(sessionProperties.session_start_date);
                    }

                  const timeOnlyStr = `${format2fieldsTime(sessionProperties.session_start_hour, sessionProperties.session_start_minute)} - ${format2fieldsTime(sessionProperties.session_end_hour, sessionProperties.session_end_minute)}`;

                  let buttonHTML = "";
                  let tags = "";
                  let external_registration_link = programProperties.external_registration_link || "";
                  if (!external_registration_link) {
                    external_registration_link =
                      programProperties.age === "adult"
                        ? "https://api.leadconnectorhq.com/widget/form/8TvNKgfffWCsUdSIb3N4"
                        : "https://api.leadconnectorhq.com/widget/form/HzInBloDoYa6iNmmXehJ";
                  }

                  const visibleNow = (startVisible && endVisible && now >= startVisible && now <= endVisible);
                  if (visibleNow) {
                    const disabled = (sessionProperties.allow_waitlist !== 'yes' && slotsFilled >= slotsAvailable) ? 'disabled="true"' : '';
                    const waitlistAvailable = sessionProperties.allow_waitlist === 'yes' && item.isWaitlist;
                    if(waitlistAvailable || disabled) {
                        console.log('has waitlist', {
                            sessionProperties,
                            slotsFilled,
                            slotsAvailable,
                            isWaitlist: item.isWaitlist
                        })
                    }
                    const disableMessage = disabled ? " (Full)" : "";
                    buttonHTML = `
                      <button style="
                        background-color: #fe074e;
                        color: white;
                        padding: 12px 20px;
                        border: none;
                        border-radius: 4px;
                        font-weight: bold;
                        font-size: 14px;
                        cursor: pointer;
                        margin-bottom: 5px;
                      " ${disabled}
                      onclick="window.location.href='${external_registration_link}?leagueSessionId=${item.id}'">
                        Register${waitlistAvailable ? ' (Waitlist)' : disableMessage}
                      </button>`;

                    if (startDate && now >= startDate) tags += formatLabel("Late Registration Available");
                    if (startVisible && startVisible <= nextWeek && startVisible >= now) tags += formatLabel("Registration Now Open");
                    if (startDate && startDate <= nextWeek && startDate >= now) tags += formatLabel("Starting Soon!");
                  } else if(item.lateRegistration) {
                    const subject = `${sessionProperties.session_name} - ${sessionProperties.session_start_date}`
                    tags += formatLabel("Late Registration Available");
                     buttonHTML = `
                      <button style="
                        background-color: #fe074e;
                        color: white;
                        padding: 12px 20px;
                        border: none;
                        border-radius: 4px;
                        font-weight: bold;
                        font-size: 14px;
                        cursor: pointer;
                        margin-bottom: 5px;"
                        onclick="window.location.href='mailto:programs@momentumvolleyball.ca?subject=${encodeURIComponent(subject)}'"
                        >
                        Register
                      </button>`;
                  } else {
                    tags = formatLabel("Registration Closed");
                  }

                  const location = {
                    name: locationProperties.location_name || "",
                    address: locationProperties.address || "",
                    city: locationProperties.city || "",
                    province: locationProperties.province || "",
                    postal_code: locationProperties.postal_code || "",
                    additional_info: locationProperties.additional_information || "",
                  };

                  // IDs must be unique across the page → prefix with SUFFIX
                  const accordionId = `accordion-${SUFFIX}-${index}-${item.id}`;
                  const inneraccordionId = `${accordionId}-inner`;

                  return `
        <div style="background:#333333; padding:24px; margin:12px 0; border-radius:8px; box-shadow:0 0 8px rgba(0,0,0,0.3); color:white;">
          <div style="display:flex; justify-content:space-between; align-items:center; flex-wrap:wrap;">
            <div style="flex:1; min-width:250px; margin-right:20px; border-radius:10px 10px 0 0; padding:10px;">
              <div style="font-weight:bold; font-size:18px;">
                <span>${sessionProperties.session_name || ""}</span>
                <a href="" onclick="event.preventDefault();window['toggleAccordion_${SUFFIX}']('${accordionId}')" style="text-decoration:none; width:100%; text-align:center; margin:0 auto; font-size:12px; font-weight:normal; color:#fe074e;">&nbsp;&nbsp; More Info <span style="font-size:12px;">▾</span></a>
              </div>
              <div style="margin-top:6px; font-weight:300; font-size:14px;">
                ${dateOnlyStr}${tags}
              </div>
            </div>
            <div style="text-align:right;display: flex; justify-content: flex-end;">
              ${buttonHTML}
            </div>
          </div>

          <div id="${accordionId}" style="display:none; margin-top:10px; padding-bottom:10px; padding-left:10px; font-size:14px; color:#000; background:#fff;">
            <div style="padding-top:10px; font-size:14px;">${info}</div>
            <div style="margin-top:6px; font-size:14px;">Cost: $${cost}</div>
            ${programProperties.show_slots === 'yes' ? `<div style="margin-top:6px; font-size:14px;">Slots: ${slotsFilled} / ${slotsAvailable}</div>` : ''}
            <div style="margin-top:6px; font-size:14px;">${timeOnlyStr} · ${sessionProperties.repeating || ""}</div>

            <div onclick="window['toggleInnerAccordion_${SUFFIX}']('${inneraccordionId}')" style="margin-top:16px; cursor:pointer; font-weight:bold; font-size:16px; color:#fe074e; display:flex; align-items:center;">
              ${location.name}
              <span style="font-size:20px;">▾</span>
            </div>
            <div id="${inneraccordionId}" style="display:none; margin-top:10px; padding-left:10px; font-size:14px; color:#000; background:#fff;">
              <div style="padding:2px 0px"><strong>Address:</strong> ${location.address}</div>
              <div style="padding:2px 0px"><strong>City:</strong> ${location.city}, ${location.province}, ${location.postal_code}</div>
              <div style="padding:2px 0px"><strong>Additional Info:</strong> ${location.additional_info}</div>
            </div>
          </div>
        </div>`;
                })
                .join("");

              return `
            <div style="margin-bottom:30px;border-left: 2px solid #fe074e; padding-left: 10px;background-color: rgba(255,255,255,0.05)">
        
        <div style="
  padding: 12px 16px;
  margin: 12px 0 20px 0;
  font-size: 15px;
  line-height: 1.5;
  color: #ddd;
  box-shadow: inset 0 0 8px rgba(0,0,0,0.2);
">
<h3 style="color:#ccc; font-size:28px; margin-top:20px; font-weight:700; font-family:'Titillium Web', sans-serif;">${programName}</h3>
  ${programInfo}
</div>
        ${itemsHTML}
      </div>`;
            })
            .join("");

          return `
    <div style="margin-bottom:50px;">
      <h2 style="color:white; font-size:40px; margin-bottom:10px; text-align:center; font-weight:700;">
        <span style="text-decoration:underline; text-decoration-color:#fe074e; text-underline-offset:8px; font-family:'Titillium Web', sans-serif;">${cityName}</span>
      </h2>
      ${programBlocks}
    </div>`;
        })
        .join("");

      container.innerHTML = output;
    } catch (err) {
      console.error("Error fetching programs:", err);
      container.innerHTML = "<p style='color:red;'>Failed to load data.</p>";
    }
  };

  // === 4) Per-instance DOM ready ===
  if (document.readyState === "loading") {
    document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", window["loadPrograms_" + SUFFIX]);
  } else {
    window["loadPrograms_" + SUFFIX]();
  }
})();
</script>

c-wrapper"><!----><!----><!----><div class="heading-TUO5oKjiLT text-output cheading-TUO5oKjiLT none noBorder radius0 none" data-animation-class style=""><div><h1><strong>Frequently Asked Questions</strong></h1></div></div><!----><!----><!----><span></span><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----></div><!--]--><!--[--><div id="faq-tNnQQahrfX" class="c-faq c-wrapper faq-tNnQQahrfX"><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><span></span><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><div class="hl-faq cfaq-tNnQQahrfX noBorder radius0 none none"><!----><!--[--><div class="faq-separated-child hl-faq-child"><div class="hl-faq-child-heading"><div class="hl-faq-child-head"><!----><span class="hl-faq-child-heading-text"><h4>What is your Refund Policy?</h4></span></div><i class="hl-faq-child-heading-icon right fa"></i></div><div style="height:0;padding:0;opacity:0;" class="hl-faq-child-panel"><span class="hl-faq-child-item-text item-text"><p>Your registration fee is refundable in full if we cannot confirm your registration. <br>Your registration fee is refundable in full (minus credit card fees) if a request is received in writing by email more than 2 months in advance of the program start date. <br>Your registration fee is refundable up to 50% (minus credit card fees) if a request is received in writing by email more than 1 month in advance of the program start date. <br>Your registration fee is refundable up to 25% (minus credit card fees) if a request is received in writing by email up to 2 weeks prior to the first day of the registered program.</p><p>There are no refunds within 2 weeks of a program’s start date.</p><p>Registrations received within the above-listed deadlines will immediately be subject to the same policy, therefore if you register within two weeks of a program's start date, your registration fee is required in full to confirm your application, and there are no refunds.</p><p>Our fees are inclusive for a full camp week or program season, and not day-by-day. Refunds will not be granted for days or sessions missed, or an early departure from a program.</p></span><!----><!----></div></div><div class="faq-separated-child hl-faq-child"><div class="hl-faq-child-heading"><div class="hl-faq-child-head"><!----><span class="hl-faq-child-heading-text"><h4>What is your Weather Policy?</h4></span></div><i class="hl-faq-child-heading-icon right fa"></i></div><div style="height:0;padding:0;opacity:0;" class="hl-faq-child-panel"><span class="hl-faq-child-item-text item-text"><p>We are open if our facilities are open! If there is a permit cancellation, we will notify our customers ASAP through email regarding the closed date, however Momentum operates as long as our facilities are open.</p></span><!----><!----></div></div><div class="faq-separated-child hl-faq-child"><div class="hl-faq-child-heading"><div class="hl-faq-child-head"><!----><span class="hl-faq-child-heading-text"><h4>Are there Make-Up Sessions for Missed Dates?</h4></span></div><i class="hl-faq-child-heading-icon right fa"></i></div><div style="height:0;padding:0;opacity:0;" class="hl-faq-child-panel"><span class="hl-faq-child-item-text item-text"><p>No, we do not offer make-up sessions for dates missed. </p></span><!----><!----></div></div><div class="faq-separated-child hl-faq-child"><div class="hl-faq-child-heading"><div class="hl-faq-child-head"><!----><span class="hl-faq-child-heading-text"><h4>Where are the locations?</h4></span></div><i class="hl-faq-child-heading-icon right fa"></i></div><div style="height:0;padding:0;opacity:0;" class="hl-faq-child-panel"><span class="hl-faq-child-item-text item-text"><p><strong>Central Toronto:&nbsp;</strong></p><p><strong>The York School – Main Campus: 1320 Yonge St., Toronto, ON</strong></p><p>Enter on the northeast corner of the building, located at the corner of Farnham Ave. &amp; Yonge St. There is a staircase that runs upstairs from Farnham Ave. to the north side of the building, and this is our main entrance for all programs at the school. There are parking options throughout the neighbourhood and along Yonge St. in the evenings. There are a few close-by Green P options, a few churches and several private garages as well. St. Clair subway station is about a 4 minute walk north of the school, and Summerhill subway station is a 10 minute walk south of the school.</p><p></p><p><strong>North York Hard Court:</strong></p><p><strong>Toronto Volleyball Centre – 75 Carl Hall Rd. in Downsview Park, North York, ON</strong></p><p>Toronto Volleyball Centre is located inside The Hangar Sports &amp; Events Centre. Enter through the main doors for The Hangar, and you will find the volleyball courts located to your left just past the ball hockey rink. Parking is free in the lot surrounding the building. Downsview Park is the closest subway station, and is a 12-minute walk north of the facility. There is also a GO Train stop at the same station that runs south to Union station and north to Aurora.</p><p></p><p><strong>North York Sand/Beach Court:</strong></p><p><strong>Volleyball Canada High Performance Beach Volleyball Centre - 75 Carl Hall Rd. Unit 3, North York, ON</strong></p><p>NOTE that this is a DIFFERENT LOCATION from our indoor programs! The Volleyball Canada facility is located on the North side of 75 Carl Hall Rd. and Unit 3 is the furthest unit west towards the hockey arena. Look for the Volleyball Canada logos on the door and front of the building. Washrooms and change rooms are located inside and are available to use.</p><p></p><p><strong>Etobicoke:&nbsp;</strong></p><p><strong>Kings Court Etobicoke – 1589 The Queensway #4, Etobicoke, ON</strong></p><p>Enter on the south side of the building, located off the main road behind the KIA dealership, and all the way to the back as far as the lane goes. The main entrance is a single door to the right of the “Kings Court” sign. There is ample free parking in front and around the building. The nearest bus stop is at Atomic Ave. which is on the same block as the facility.</p><p></p><p><strong>Kincardine Indoor:</strong></p><p><strong>Davidson Centre - 601 Durham St, Kincardine, ON</strong></p><p>Enter through the main doors, and turn right down the short flight of stairs. The gym is directly behind the front desk at the main entrance. Upstairs is available for mezzanine seating, where parents can watch with plenty of places to sit.</p><p></p><p><strong>Kincardine Beach:</strong></p><p><strong>Station Beach - 249 Station Beach Rd, Kincardine, ON</strong></p><p>The beach volleyball courts are visible as soon as you turn onto Station Beach Rd. and parking is available next to the courts. There are bathrooms next to the courts and a water fountain. A covered gazebo and Momentum's 10' x 10' tent are above several picnic tables for snack breaks.</p><p></p><p><strong>Wiarton:</strong></p><p><strong>Peninsula Shores District School - 115 George St. Wiarton, ON</strong></p><p>Enter through the main doors of the school, towards the north end of the entrance area. The gym is across the hall from the auditorium, and follows the north hallway that runs off the main entrance area. You should not have to open any doors inside until you get to the gym.</p><p></p><p><strong>Owen Sound:</strong></p><p><strong>Timothy Christian School - 1735 4th Ave W, Owen Sound, ON</strong></p><p>Enter through the main doors on 17th St. West, and the gym will be on your right.</p><p></p><p><strong>Hanover:</strong></p><p><strong>John Diefenbaker Secondary School - 201 18th Ave, Hanover, ON</strong></p><p>Enter through the main doors.</p></span><!----><!----></div></div><!--]--></div><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----></div><!--]--><!--]--></div><!----><!----><!----><!----><span></span><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----></div><!--]--><!--]--></div><!----><!----><!----><!----><span></span><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----></div><!--]--><!--]--></div><!----><!----><!----><!----><span></span><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----></div><!--]--><!--[--><div
